$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / While_Loops_Printing1

::While Loops Printing Level 1 #000::
What is the following output of the code?
<pre>int d = 25;
while (d < 35)
\{
	cout << d << ' ';
	d += 5;
\}
</pre>	{
	=25 30 
	~30 
	~30 35 
	~25 
	~25 30 35 
	}

	}

while (i <= 5)
\{
	cout << i << ' ';
	i += 1;
\}
</pre>	{
	=2 3 4 5 
	~3 4 5 
	~3 4 5 6 
	~2 3 4 
	~2 3 4 5 6 
	}

</pre>	{

	~20 30 40 50 60 
	}

::While Loops Printing Level 2 #666::

\{

\}
</pre>	{
	=74 64 54 44 
	~64 54 44 
	~64 54 44 34 
	~74 64 54 
	~74 64 54 44 34 
	}

::While Loops Printing Level 3 #667::
What is the following output of the code?
<pre>int a = 203;
while (a > 2)
\{
	cout << a << ' ';
	a /= 10;
\}
</pre>	{
	=203 20 
	~20 
	~20 2 
	~203 
	~203 20 2 
	}
